if (window.top !== window.self) {
    window.top.location = window.self.location;

var waitFor = function (condition, retryTime, maxRetries, success, failure) {

    failure = failure || function () {};

    var retried = 0;
    var timer = null;

    var waitForImpl = function () {
        if (condition()) {
            window.clearTimeout(timer);
            success();
        } else if (retried &gt; maxRetries) {
            window.clearTimeout(timer);
            failure();
        } else {
            retried++;
            timer = window.setTimeout(waitForImpl, retryTime);
        }
    };

    waitForImpl();
};

var appendScriptTag = function(src, async) {

    var s = document.createElement( 'script' );
    s.setAttribute( 'src', src );
    if (async) {

        s.setAttribute("async", "");
    }
    document.body.appendChild( s );
